Copying only happens in 1 direction.\r\n\r\nPossible data storage devices are:\r\n- A hard drive of the computer.\r\n- An external USB storage device: USB sticks, USB hard drives or SSD drives.\r\n- A network storage station: a shared network drive.\r\n- A cloud storage location: OneDrive, DropBox, ..\r\n\r\nAll backup / synchronization jobs can run automatically at a configured time or can be started manually.\r\n\r\nCopying happens incrementaly: only those folders and files are copied that are new or have changed since the last backup. That gives you the possibility to exclude certain sub-folders, hidden folders, etc.\r\n\r\nYou can copy in 2 ways: \r\n- By mirroring: This method ensures that the folders and files on the storage medium are an exact copy of those on the source. If files disappear on the source location, they also disappear on the target location.\r\n- By blind copying: This method also copies all new and changed files, but files that are no longer present at the source location are not deleted on the target medium.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NJ46SX7X90P","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Python 3.7","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.46763.13683872343053742.6c777826-d7ea-427a-942f-7dbfb474c121.7cd9c7f0-9cd8-4686-bd82-f7f4a18971ec","Height":150,"Width":150,"BackgroundColor":"transparent","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Безплатно","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["PythonSoftwareFoundation.Python.3.7_qbz5n2kfra8p0"],"ContentIds":["4722e0c1-673f-f65d-ff2f-75137d1b1edf"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"Компютър","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Python is an easy to learn, powerful programming language.
